–°–µ—Ä–≥—ñ–π –ú.: To have the items craft faster you reduce the value, the closer to 0, the shorter the crafting time. If you would want the crafting to go slower you increase the number over 100. A few examples: /rate 0 results in instant-craft /rate 50 results in half-craft /rate 100 results in normal-craft /rate 150 results in 50% extra crafting time /rate 200 results in double-craft
